56 bool HardwareLoopInfo::canAnalyze(LoopInfo &LI) { 0
57 // If the loop has irreducible control flow, it can not be converted to ----
58 // Hardware loop. ----
59 LoopBlocksRPO RPOT(L); 0
60 RPOT.perform(&LI); 0
61 if (containsIrreducibleCFG(RPOT, LI)) 0
62 return false; 0
63 return true; 0
64 } 0

69 : II(dyn_cast(&CI)), RetTy(CI.getType()), IID(Id), 0

77 FunctionType *FTy = CI.getCalledFunction()->getFunctionType(); 0
78 ParamTys.insert(ParamTys.begin(), FTy->param_begin(), FTy->param_end()); 0
79 } 0

111 HardwareLoopInfo::HardwareLoopInfo(Loop *L) : L(L) { 0
112 // Match default options: ----
113 // - hardware-loop-counter-bitwidth = 32 ----
114 // - hardware-loop-decrement = 1 ----
115 CountType = Type::getInt32Ty(L->getHeader()->getContext()); 0
116 LoopDecrement = ConstantInt::get(CountType, 1); 0
117 } 0
118 ----
119 bool HardwareLoopInfo::isHardwareLoopCandidate(ScalarEvolution &SE, 0
120 LoopInfo &LI, DominatorTree &DT, ----
121 bool ForceNestedLoop, ----
122 bool ForceHardwareLoopPHI) { ----
123 SmallVector ExitingBlocks; 0
124 L->getExitingBlocks(ExitingBlocks); 0
125 ----
126 for (BasicBlock *BB : ExitingBlocks) { 0
127 // If we pass the updated counter back through a phi, we need to know ----
128 // which latch the updated value will be coming from. ----
129 if (!L->isLoopLatch(BB)) { 0
130 if (ForceHardwareLoopPHI || CounterInReg) 0
131 continue; 0
132 } ----
133 ----
134 const SCEV *EC = SE.getExitCount(L, BB); 0
135 if (isa(EC)) 0
136 continue; 0
137 if (const SCEVConstant *ConstEC = dyn_cast(EC)) { 0
138 if (ConstEC->getValue()->isZero()) 0
139 continue; 0
140 } else if (!SE.isLoopInvariant(EC, L)) 0
141 continue; 0
142 ----
143 if (SE.getTypeSizeInBits(EC->getType()) > CountType->getBitWidth()) 0
144 continue; 0
145 ----
146 // If this exiting block is contained in a nested loop, it is not eligible ----
147 // for insertion of the branch-and-decrement since the inner loop would ----
148 // end up messing up the value in the CTR. ----
149 if (!IsNestingLegal && LI.getLoopFor(BB) != L && !ForceNestedLoop) 0
150 continue; 0
151 ----
152 // We now have a loop-invariant count of loop iterations (which is not the ----
153 // constant zero) for which we know that this loop will not exit via this ----
154 // existing block. ----
155 ----
156 // We need to make sure that this block will run on every loop iteration. ----
157 // For this to be true, we must dominate all blocks with backedges. Such ----
158 // blocks are in-loop predecessors to the header block. ----
159 bool NotAlways = false; 0
160 for (BasicBlock *Pred : predecessors(L->getHeader())) { 0
161 if (!L->contains(Pred)) 0
162 continue; 0
163 ----
164 if (!DT.dominates(BB, Pred)) { 0
165 NotAlways = true; 0
166 break; 0
167 } ----
168 } ----
169 ----
170 if (NotAlways) 0
171 continue; 0
172 ----
173 // Make sure this blocks ends with a conditional branch. ----
174 Instruction *TI = BB->getTerminator(); 0
175 if (!TI) 0
176 continue; 0
177 ----
178 if (BranchInst *BI = dyn_cast(TI)) { 0
179 if (!BI->isConditional()) 0
180 continue; 0
181 ----
182 ExitBranch = BI; 0
183 } else ----
184 continue; 0
185 ----
186 // Note that this block may not be the loop latch block, even if the loop ----
187 // has a latch block. ----
188 ExitBlock = BB; 0
189 ExitCount = EC; 0
190 break; 0
191 } ----
192 ----
193 if (!ExitBlock) 0
194 return false; 0
195 return true; 0
196 } 0

771 ----
772 TargetTransformInfo::OperandValueInfo ----
773 TargetTransformInfo::getOperandInfo(const Value *V) { 0
774 OperandValueKind OpInfo = OK_AnyValue; 0
775 OperandValueProperties OpProps = OP_None; 0
776 ----
777 if (isa(V) || isa(V)) { 0
778 if (const auto *CI = dyn_cast(V)) { 0
779 if (CI->getValue().isPowerOf2()) 0
780 OpProps = OP_PowerOf2; 0
781 else if (CI->getValue().isNegatedPowerOf2()) 0
782 OpProps = OP_NegatedPowerOf2; 0
783 } ----
784 return {OK_UniformConstantValue, OpProps}; 0
785 } ----
786 ----
787 // A broadcast shuffle creates a uniform value. ----
788 // TODO: Add support for non-zero index broadcasts. ----
789 // TODO: Add support for different source vector width. ----
790 if (const auto *ShuffleInst = dyn_cast(V)) 0
791 if (ShuffleInst->isZeroEltSplat()) 0
792 OpInfo = OK_UniformValue; 0
793 ----
794 const Value *Splat = getSplatValue(V); 0
795 ----
796 // Check for a splat of a constant or for a non uniform vector of constants ----
797 // and check if the constant(s) are all powers of two. ----
798 if (isa(V) || isa(V)) { 0
799 OpInfo = OK_NonUniformConstantValue; 0
800 if (Splat) { 0
801 OpInfo = OK_UniformConstantValue; 0
802 if (auto *CI = dyn_cast(Splat)) { 0
803 if (CI->getValue().isPowerOf2()) 0
804 OpProps = OP_PowerOf2; 0
805 else if (CI->getValue().isNegatedPowerOf2()) 0
806 OpProps = OP_NegatedPowerOf2; 0
807 } ----
808 } else if (const auto *CDS = dyn_cast(V)) { 0
809 bool AllPow2 = true, AllNegPow2 = true; 0
810 for (unsigned I = 0, E = CDS->getNumElements(); I != E; ++I) { 0
811 if (auto *CI = dyn_cast(CDS->getElementAsConstant(I))) { 0
812 AllPow2 &= CI->getValue().isPowerOf2(); 0
813 AllNegPow2 &= CI->getValue().isNegatedPowerOf2(); 0
814 if (AllPow2 || AllNegPow2) 0
815 continue; 0
816 } ----
817 AllPow2 = AllNegPow2 = false; 0
818 break; 0
819 } ----
820 OpProps = AllPow2 ? OP_PowerOf2 : OpProps; 0
821 OpProps = AllNegPow2 ? OP_NegatedPowerOf2 : OpProps; 0
822 } ----
823 } ----
824 ----
825 // Check for a splat of a uniform value. This is not loop aware, so return ----
826 // true only for the obviously uniform cases (argument, globalvalue) ----
827 if (Splat && (isa(Splat) || isa(Splat))) 0
828 OpInfo = OK_UniformValue; 0
829 ----
830 return {OpInfo, OpProps}; 0
831 } ----
832 ----
833 InstructionCost TargetTransformInfo::getArithmeticInstrCost( 0
834 unsigned Opcode, Type *Ty, TTI::TargetCostKind CostKind, ----
835 OperandValueInfo Op1Info, OperandValueInfo Op2Info, ----
836 ArrayRef Args, const Instruction *CxtI) const { ----
837 InstructionCost Cost = ----
838 TTIImpl->getArithmeticInstrCost(Opcode, Ty, CostKind, 0
839 Op1Info, Op2Info, ----
840 Args, CxtI); ----
841 assert(Cost >= 0 && "TTI should not produce negative costs!"); 0
842 return Cost; 0
843 } ----
844 ----
845 InstructionCost TargetTransformInfo::getShuffleCost( 0
846 ShuffleKind Kind, VectorType *Ty, ArrayRef Mask, ----
847 TTI::TargetCostKind CostKind, int Index, VectorType *SubTp, ----
848 ArrayRef Args) const { ----
849 InstructionCost Cost = ----
850 TTIImpl->getShuffleCost(Kind, Ty, Mask, CostKind, Index, SubTp, Args); 0
851 assert(Cost >= 0 && "TTI should not produce negative costs!"); 0
852 return Cost; 0
853 } ----
854 ----
855 TTI::CastContextHint ----
856 TargetTransformInfo::getCastContextHint(const Instruction *I) { 0
857 if (!I) 0
858 return CastContextHint::None; 0
859 ----
860 auto getLoadStoreKind = [](const Value *V, unsigned LdStOp, unsigned MaskedOp, 0
861 unsigned GatScatOp) { ----
862 const Instruction *I = dyn_cast(V); 0
863 if (!I) 0
864 return CastContextHint::None; 0
865 ----
866 if (I->getOpcode() == LdStOp) 0
867 return CastContextHint::Normal; 0
868 ----
869 if (const IntrinsicInst *II = dyn_cast(I)) { 0
870 if (II->getIntrinsicID() == MaskedOp) 0
871 return TTI::CastContextHint::Masked; 0
872 if (II->getIntrinsicID() == GatScatOp) 0
873 return TTI::CastContextHint::GatherScatter; 0
874 } ----
875 ----
876 return TTI::CastContextHint::None; 0
877 }; ----
878 ----
879 switch (I->getOpcode()) { 0
880 case Instruction::ZExt: 0
881 case Instruction::SExt: ----
882 case Instruction::FPExt: ----
883 return getLoadStoreKind(I->getOperand(0), Instruction::Load, 0
884 Intrinsic::masked_load, Intrinsic::masked_gather); 0
885 case Instruction::Trunc: 0
886 case Instruction::FPTrunc: ----
887 if (I->hasOneUse()) 0
888 return getLoadStoreKind(*I->user_begin(), Instruction::Store, 0
889 Intrinsic::masked_store, ----
890 Intrinsic::masked_scatter); 0
891 break; 0
892 default: 0
893 return CastContextHint::None; 0
894 } ----
895 ----
896 return TTI::CastContextHint::None; 0
897 } ----
898 ----
899 InstructionCost TargetTransformInfo::getCastInstrCost( 0
900 unsigned Opcode, Type *Dst, Type *Src, CastContextHint CCH, ----
901 TTI::TargetCostKind CostKind, const Instruction *I) const { ----
902 assert((I == nullptr || I->getOpcode() == Opcode) && 0
903 "Opcode should reflect passed instruction."); ----
904 InstructionCost Cost = ----
905 TTIImpl->getCastInstrCost(Opcode, Dst, Src, CCH, CostKind, I); 0
906 assert(Cost >= 0 && "TTI should not produce negative costs!"); 0
907 return Cost; 0
908 } ----

56 bool HardwareLoopInfo::canAnalyze(LoopInfo &LI) { 56 bool HardwareLoopInfo::canAnalyze(LoopInfo &LI) {
